'@/store/useProjectStore';\n// Removed srt-parser-2 dependency\n\nexport const parseSrt = (srtContent: string): 
CaptionSegment[] => {\n  // Normalize line endings and split by double blank lines\n  const normalized = 
srtContent.replace(/\\r\\n/g, '\\n').replace(/\\r/g, '\\n');\n  const blocks = normalized.split(/\\n\\n+/);\n  \n  
const segments: CaptionSegment[] = [];\n  \n  for (const block of blocks) {\n    const lines = 
block.trim().split('\\n');\n    if (lines.length >= 3) {\n      const id = lines[0].trim();\n      const timeLine = 
lines[1];\n      const textLines = lines.slice(2);\n      \n      const timeMatch = 
timeLine.match(/(\\d{1,2}:\\d{2}:\\d{2}[,.]\\d{2,3})\\s*-->\\s*(\\d{1,2}:\\d{2}:\\d{2}[,.]\\d{2,3})/);\n      \n      
if (timeMatch) {\n        const text = textLines.join(' ').replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '').trim();\n        \n        // 
Auto-detect important word\n        const words = text.split(' ').filter(w => w.trim().length > 0);\n        let 
cleanImportant = '';\n        let bestIndex = -1;\n\n        if (words.length > 0) {\n          let bestWord = 
words[0];\n          let maxScore = -100;\n\n          words.forEach((w, index) => {\n            let score = 
w.length; \n            if (index === words.length - 1) score += 3; // Punchline bonus\n            if (index === 0) 
score += 1; // Start word bonus\n            if (w.match(/[A-Z]/)) {\n              if (w === w.toUpperCase()) {\n     
           score += 5; // All caps bonus\n              } else {\n                score += 2; // Title case bonus\n    
          }\n            }\n            if (w.length <= 2) score -= 10; // Penalize stop words strongly\n            
if (w.length >= 7) score += 2; // Reward long descriptive words\n\n            if (score > maxScore) {\n              
maxScore = score;\n              bestWord = w;\n            }\n          });\n          \n          cleanImportant = 
bestWord.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim();\n          words.forEach((w, i) => {\n       
     if (w === bestWord && bestIndex === -1) {\n              bestIndex = i;\n            }\n          });\n        
}\n\n        segments.push({\n          id,\n          startTime: parseTimeToMs(timeMatch[1]),\n          endTime: 
parseTimeToMs(timeMatch[2]),\n          text,\n          highlightedWords: cleanImportant ? [cleanImportant] : [],\n   
       highlightedIndices: bestIndex !== -1 ? [bestIndex] : [],\n          originalHighlightedWords: cleanImportant ? 
[cleanImportant] : [],\n          originalHighlightedIndices: bestIndex !== -1 ? [bestIndex] : []\n        });\n      
}\n    }\n  }\n  if (segments.length > 0 && segments[0].startTime < 333) {\n    segments[0].startTime = 333;\n    if 
(segments[0].endTime <= 333) {\n      segments[0].endTime = 333 + 1000;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return segments;\n};\n\n// 
Converts \"HH:MM:SS,ms\" or \"HH:MM:SS.ms\" to milliseconds\nconst parseTimeToMs = (timeString: string): number => {\n 
 if (!timeString) return 0;\n  const parts = timeString.split(':');\n  if (parts.length !== 3) return 0;\n  const 
[hours, minutes, secondsAndMs] = parts;\n  const [seconds, ms] = secondsAndMs.split(/[,.]/);\n  \n  const h = 
parseInt(hours, 10) || 0;\n  const m = parseInt(minutes, 10) || 0;\n  const s = parseInt(seconds, 10) || 0;\n  const 
mil = parseInt(ms, 10) || 0;\n\n  return h * 3600000 + m * 60000 + s * 1000 + mil;\n};\n","/**\n * Check if a 
component has an accessibility prop\n *\n * @param {object} props\n * @returns {boolean} Whether the component has an

   if (prop.startsWith('aria-') || prop === 'role' || prop === 'title') {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return

'$1-$2').toLowerCase();\n","/**\n * Merges classes into a single string\n *\n * @param {array} classes\n * @returns

&&\n        (className as string).trim() !== '' &&\n        array.indexOf(className) === index\n      );\n    })\n

{\n      font: 'Montserrat', baseColor: '#ffffff', accentColor: '#ffffff', backgroundColor: '#ff0000', fontSize: 130, 
baseFontSizeMultiplier: 0.9, accentFontSizeMultiplier: 1.1, animationType: 'pop', displayMode: 'word', highlightStyle: 
'highlight'\n    },\n    preview: (\n      <span style={{ fontFamily: 'Montserrat', color: '#ffffff', fontSize:

{\n      font: 'Montserrat', baseColor: '#ffffff', accentColor: '#ffffff', backgroundColor: '#ffb703', fontSize: 130, 
baseFontSizeMultiplier: 1.0, accentFontSizeMultiplier: 1.1, animationType: 'none', displayMode: 'karaoke', 
highlightStyle: 'highlight'\n    },\n    preview: (\n      <span style={{ fontFamily: 'Montserrat', color: '#ffffff',

padding: '0px 4px', borderRadius: '4px' }}>WORD</span>\n      </span>\n    )\n  }\n];\n\nexport interface FontGroup 
{\n  family: string;\n  weights: { label: string; value: number; fullName: string }[];\n}\n\nconst CustomFontPicker = 
({ fonts, value, onChange, isLoading }: { fonts: FontGroup[], value: string, onChange: (v: string) => void, isLoading: 
boolean }) => {\n  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');\n  const 
[renderLimit, setRenderLimit] = useState(50);\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    const handleClick = () => 
setIsOpen(false);\n    if (isOpen) {\n       document.addEventListener('click', handleClick);\n       
setRenderLimit(50);\n    }\n    return () => document.removeEventListener('click', handleClick);\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  
const filteredFonts = fonts.filter(f => f.family.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));\n\n  const 
handleScroll = (e: React.UIEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {\n    const { scrollTop, scrollHeight, clientHeight } = 
e.currentTarget;\n    if (scrollHeight - scrollTop <= clientHeight + 100) {\n      setRenderLimit(prev => 
Math.min(prev + 50, filteredFonts.length));\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"relative\" onClick={(e) 
=> e.stopPropagation()}>\n      <button \n        onClick={() => { setIsOpen(!isOpen); setSearch(''); }}\n        
className=\"w-full flex items-center justify-between bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 text-sm 
focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500\"\n      >\n        <span 
className=\"truncate\">{value}</span>\n        <ChevronDown className=\"w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 flex-shrink-0\" />\n     
 </button>\n\n      {isOpen && (\n        <div className=\"absolute z-50 w-full mt-1 bg-gray-900 border 
border-gray-700 rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden\" style={{ maxHeight: '300px' }}>\n          <div 
className=\"p-2 border-b border-gray-700 bg-gray-800\">\n            <input \n              autoFocus\n              
className=\"w-full bg-gray-900 text-white px-3 py-1.5 text-sm rounded border border-gray-700 focus:outline-none 
focus:border-indigo-500\"\n              placeholder=\"Search fonts...\"\n              value={search}\n              
onChange={e => { setSearch(e.target.value); setRenderLimit(50); }}\n            />\n          </div>\n          <div 
className=\"overflow-y-auto flex-1\" onScroll={handleScroll}>\n            {isLoading && <div className=\"p-4 text-xs 
text-gray-400 text-center\">Loading Fonts...</div>}\n            \n            {filteredFonts.slice(0, 
renderLimit).map((font) => (\n                <button\n                  key={font.family}\n                  
onClick={() => {\n                    onChange(font.family);\n                    setIsOpen(false);\n                  
}}\n                  className={`w-full text-left px-4 py-3 hover:bg-indigo-600/20 flex items-center justify-between 
border-b border-gray-700/50 last:border-b-0 transition-colors ${value === font.family ? 'bg-indigo-600/30 text-white' 
: 'text-gray-300'}`}\n                >\n                  <span style={{ fontFamily: `\"${font.family}\", 
sans-serif`, fontSize: '16px' }}>{font.family}</span>\n                  {value === font.family && <Check 
className=\"w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400\" />}\n                </button>\n            ))}\n\n            {!isLoading && 
filteredFonts.length === 0 && (\n              <div className=\"p-4 text-xs text-gray-400 text-center\">No fonts 
found</div>\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nconst 
CustomColorPicker = ({ \n  label, \n  value, \n  onChange, \n  savedColors, \n  onSave, \n  onRemove \n}: { \n  label: 
string, \n  value: string, \n  onChange: (c: string) => void, \n  savedColors: string[], \n  onSave: (c: string) => 
void, \n  onRemove: (c: string) => void \n}) => {\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex flex-col gap-1\">\n      <div 
className=\"flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[16px] mb-1\">\n        <label className=\"text-[10px] leading-tight 
text-gray-400 font-medium flex-1 truncate\" title={label}>{label}</label>\n        <button \n          onClick={() => 
onSave(value)}\n          className=\"shrink-0 text-[12px] font-bold w-4 h-4 flex items-center justify-center 
bg-indigo-500/20 hover:bg-indigo-500/40 text-indigo-300 rounded border border-indigo-500/30 transition leading-none 
cursor-pointer\"\n          title=\"Save this color to your palette\"\n        >\n          +\n        </button>\n     
 </div>\n      <input \n        type=\"color\" \n        value={value}\n        onChange={(e) => 
onChange(e.target.value)}\n        className=\"w-full h-10 rounded-lg cursor-pointer bg-gray-900 border 
border-gray-700 p-1\"\n      />\n      {savedColors.length > 0 && (\n        <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-1 
mt-1\">\n          {savedColors.map((c, i) => (\n            <div \n              key={`${c}-${i}`}\n              
onClick={() => onChange(c)}\n              onContextMenu={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); onRemove(c); }}\n              
className=\"w-4 h-4 rounded-sm border border-gray-600 cursor-pointer hover:scale-110 transition-transform\"\n          
    style={{ backgroundColor: c }}\n              title={`${c} (Right-click to remove)`}\n            />\n          
))}\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport const StylePanel = () => {\n  const { \n    styleConfig: 
globalStyleConfig, \n    setStyleConfig, \n    individualStylingEnabled, \n    setIndividualStylingEnabled,\n    
selectedCaptionId, \n    setSelectedCaptionId, \n    setHighlightSimilar,\n    captions, \n    setCaptions,\n    
updateCaptionSegment,\n    customPresets,\n    saveCustomPreset,\n    deleteCustomPreset,\n    importCustomPresets,\n  
  showTextBoxBorder,\n    setShowTextBoxBorder,\n    customColors,\n    addCustomColor,\n    removeCustomColor\n  } = 
useProjectStore();\n\n  const handleExportPresets = () => {\n    if (customPresets.length === 0) return;\n    const 
dataStr = JSON.stringify(customPresets, null, 2);\n    const blob = new Blob([dataStr], { type: \"application/json\" 
});\n    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);\n    const a = document.createElement('a');\n    a.href = url;\n    
a.download = \"auto-caps-presets.json\";\n    document.body.appendChild(a);\n    a.click();\n    
document.body.removeChild(a);\n    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);\n  };\n\n  const handleImportPresets = (e: 
React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n    const 
reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = (event) => {\n      try {\n        const json = 
JSON.parse(event.target?.result as string);\n        if (Array.isArray(json)) {\n          
importCustomPresets(json);\n          alert(\"Successfully imported presets!\");\n        } else {\n          
alert(\"Invalid preset file format.\");\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        alert(\"Failed to parse preset 
file.\");\n      }\n    };\n    reader.readAsText(file);\n    // clear input value so the same file can be uploaded 
again if needed\n    e.target.value = '';\n  };\n\n  const selectedCaption = selectedCaptionId ? captions.find(c => 
c.id === selectedCaptionId) : null;\n  const isEditingIndividual = individualStylingEnabled && !!selectedCaption;\n\n  
// The active config to display in the UI\n  const styleConfig = isEditingIndividual\n    ? { ...globalStyleConfig, 
...(selectedCaption!.customStyle || {}) }\n    : globalStyleConfig;\n\n  const [systemFonts, setSystemFonts] = 
useState<FontGroup[]>(() => {\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {\n      const cached = 
localStorage.getItem('systemFontsCache');\n      if (cached) {\n        try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch(e) 
{}\n      }\n    }\n    return [];\n  });\n  const [isLoadingFonts, setIsLoadingFonts] = useState(systemFonts.length 
=== 0);\n  const [presetTab, setPresetTab] = useState<'system'|'custom'>('system');\n  const [newPresetName, 
setNewPresetName] = useState('');\n  const [openPanels, setOpenPanels] = useState<string[]>([\"ðŸ’¡ Layout\"]);\n  
const [autoCollapsePanels, setAutoCollapsePanels] = useState(false);\n  const [presetContextMenu, 
setPresetContextMenu] = useState<{x: number, y: number, presetName: string} | null>(null);\n  const [showResetModal, 
setShowResetModal] = useState(false);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {\n      
setAutoCollapsePanels(localStorage.getItem('autoCollapsePanels') === 'true');\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => 
{\n    const handleClick = () => setPresetContextMenu(null);\n    if (presetContextMenu) {\n      
document.addEventListener('click', handleClick);\n    }\n    return () => document.removeEventListener('click', 
handleClick);\n  }, [presetContextMenu]);\n  \n  const togglePanel = (panelName: string) => {\n    if 
(autoCollapsePanels) {\n      if (openPanels.includes(panelName)) {\n        setOpenPanels([]);\n      } else {\n      
  setOpenPanels([panelName]);\n      }\n    } else {\n      if (openPanels.includes(panelName)) {\n        
setOpenPanels(openPanels.filter(p => p !== panelName));\n      } else {\n        setOpenPanels([...openPanels, 
panelName]);\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleToggleAutoCollapse = () => {\n    const newVal = 
!autoCollapsePanels;\n    setAutoCollapsePanels(newVal);\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {\n      
localStorage.setItem('autoCollapsePanels', newVal.toString());\n    }\n    if (newVal && openPanels.length > 1) {\n    
  setOpenPanels([openPanels[0]]);\n    }\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetch('/api/fonts')\n      .then(res => 
res.json())\n      .then(data => {\n        if (data.fontsGrouped) {\n          setSystemFonts(data.fontsGrouped);\n   
       if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {\n            localStorage.setItem('systemFontsCache',

.catch(err => {\n        console.error('Failed to auto-load system fonts:', err);\n        setIsLoadingFonts(false);\n 
     });\n  }, []);\n\n  const handleUpdate = (updates: Partial<StyleConfig>) => {\n    if (isEditingIndividual) {\n   
   updateCaptionSegment(selectedCaptionId!, { \n        customStyle: { ...(selectedCaption!.customStyle || {}), 
...updates } \n      });\n    } else {\n      // If a setting is manually changed, detach from the active preset\n     
 const newConfig = { ...updates };\n      if (!('activePreset' in updates)) {\n        newConfig.activePreset = 
undefined;\n      }\n      setStyleConfig(newConfig);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"bg-gray-800

 className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-1 rounded transition border ${autoCollapsePanels ? 'bg-indigo-900/40 
border-indigo-500/50 text-indigo-300' : 'bg-gray-700/50 border-gray-600/50 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-200'}`}\n     
       title=\"When ON, opening a panel automatically closes others\"\n          >\n            Auto Collapse: 
{autoCollapsePanels ? 'ON' : 'OFF'}\n          </button>\n          <button \n            onClick={() =>

text-gray-200 transition font-medium\"\n            title=\"Reset Options\"\n          >\n            Reset\n          
</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {isEditingIndividual ? (\n        <div className=\"bg-indigo-600/20

justify-between\">\n          <span>Editing Individual Caption</span>\n          <button \n            onClick={() => 
updateCaptionSegment(selectedCaptionId!, { customStyle: {} })}\n            className=\"bg-indigo-500/30 
hover:bg-indigo-500/50 px-2 py-1 rounded text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider\"\n          >\n            Reset\n      
    </button>\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"bg-gray-700/30 text-gray-400 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg 
text-xs font-semibold mb-4 text-center\">\n          Editing Global Styles (All Captions)\n        </div>\n      
)}\n\n      <AccordionItem title=\"âš™ï¸ Video Settings\" isOpen={openPanels.includes(\"Video Settings\")}

     {(['9:16', '16:9'] as const).map((ratio) => (\n              <button\n                key={ratio}\n

      >\n            System\n          </button>\n          <button\n            onClick={() =>

       }\n                      handleUpdate(updates);\n                    }}\n                    className=\"w-full

             </div>\n              );\n            }\n            return null;\n          })()}\n        </div>\n\n

       <button\n              onClick={() => handleUpdate({ enableHighlightFont: !styleConfig.enableHighlightFont 
})}\n              className={`w-10 h-5 rounded-full relative transition-colors ${styleConfig.enableHighlightFont ?

bg-white rounded-full transition-transform ${styleConfig.enableHighlightFont ? 'translate-x-5' : 'translate-x-0'}`} 
/>\n            </button>\n          </label>\n          \n          {styleConfig.enableHighlightFont && (\n           
 <div className=\"mt-2 bg-gray-900/50 p-3 rounded-lg border border-gray-700\">\n              <label

         fonts={systemFonts}\n                value={styleConfig.highlightFont}\n                onChange={(v) => {\n  
                 const fontGroup = systemFonts.find(f => f.family === v);\n                   let newWeight = 
styleConfig.highlightFontWeight;\n                   if (fontGroup && fontGroup.weights.length > 0) {\n                
     if (!fontGroup.weights.find(w => w.value === newWeight)) {\n                       newWeight = 
fontGroup.weights.find(w => w.value === 400)?.value || fontGroup.weights[0].value;\n                     }\n

createLucideIcon('book-open', __iconNode);\n\nexport default BookOpen;\n","'use client';\n\nimport React, { useRef, 
useEffect, useState } from 'react';\nimport { Player } from '@remotion/player';\nimport type { PlayerRef } from

=> {\n  const { videoUrl, captions, styleConfig, fps, videoDuration, undo, redo, pastCaptions, futureCaptions,

[editingCaptionText, setEditingCaptionText] = useState('');\n  \n  const [isLeftPanelOpen, setIsLeftPanelOpen] =

useState(false);\n  useEffect(() => {\n    setMounted(true);\n  }, []);\n\n  const toggleHighlight = (captionId: 
string, word: string, wordIndex: number) => {\n    const caption = captions.find(c => c.id === captionId);\n    if 
(!caption) return;\n    \n    // Clean punctuation for matching but store the clean version\n    const cleanWord = 
word.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim();\n    \n    if (highlightSimilar) {\n      let 
isCurrentlyHighlighted = false;\n      const currentIndices = caption.highlightedIndices;\n      if (currentIndices) 
{\n        isCurrentlyHighlighted = currentIndices.includes(wordIndex);\n      } else {\n        
isCurrentlyHighlighted = caption.highlightedWords.some(hw => hw.toLowerCase() === cleanWord);\n      }\n\n      const 
newCaptions = captions.map(cap => {\n        let capCurrentIndices = cap.highlightedIndices;\n        if 
(!capCurrentIndices) {\n          capCurrentIndices = [];\n          const wordsArr = cap.text.split(' ');\n          
wordsArr.forEach((w, i) => {\n            const cw = w.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, 
'').toLowerCase().trim();\n            if (cap.highlightedWords.some(hw => hw.toLowerCase() === cw)) {\n              
capCurrentIndices!.push(i);\n            }\n          });\n        }\n        \n        let newHighlights = 
[...cap.highlightedWords];\n        let newHighlightIndices = [...capCurrentIndices];\n\n        if 
(isCurrentlyHighlighted) {\n          newHighlights = newHighlights.filter(w => w.toLowerCase() !== cleanWord);\n      
    const wordsArr = cap.text.split(' ');\n          wordsArr.forEach((w, i) => {\n            if 
(w.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim() === cleanWord) {\n              newHighlightIndices 
= newHighlightIndices.filter(idx => idx !== i);\n            }\n          });\n        } else {\n          
newHighlights.push(cleanWord);\n          const wordsArr = cap.text.split(' ');\n          wordsArr.forEach((w, i) => 
{\n            if (w.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim() === cleanWord && 
!newHighlightIndices.includes(i)) {\n              newHighlightIndices.push(i);\n            }\n          });\n        
}\n        \n        return { ...cap, highlightedWords: newHighlights, highlightedIndices: newHighlightIndices };\n    
  });\n      \n      setCaptions(newCaptions);\n    } else {\n      // Normalize indices if they don't exist\n      
let currentIndices = caption.highlightedIndices;\n      if (!currentIndices) {\n        currentIndices = [];\n        
const wordsArr = caption.text.split(' ');\n        wordsArr.forEach((w, i) => {\n          const cw = 
w.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim();\n          if (caption.highlightedWords.some(hw => 
hw.toLowerCase() === cw)) {\n            currentIndices!.push(i);\n          }\n        });\n      }\n\n      let 
newHighlights = [...caption.highlightedWords];\n      let newHighlightIndices = [...currentIndices];\n      \n      if 
(newHighlightIndices.includes(wordIndex)) {\n        newHighlightIndices = newHighlightIndices.filter(idx => idx !== 
wordIndex);\n        // Optional: remove from newHighlights if no more indices of this word exist\n        const 
wordsArr = caption.text.split(' ');\n        const hasMoreOfThisWord = newHighlightIndices.some(idx => 
wordsArr[idx].replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim() === cleanWord);\n        if 
(!hasMoreOfThisWord) {\n          newHighlights = newHighlights.filter(w => w.toLowerCase() !== cleanWord);\n        
}\n      } else {\n        newHighlightIndices.push(wordIndex);\n        if (!newHighlights.some(w => w.toLowerCase() 
=== cleanWord)) {\n          newHighlights.push(cleanWord);\n        }\n      }\n      \n      
updateCaptionSegment(captionId, { highlightedWords: newHighlights, highlightedIndices: newHighlightIndices });\n    
}\n  };\n\n  const autoHighlightAll = () => {\n    const newCaptions = captions.map(cap => {\n      const words = 
cap.text.split(' ').filter(w => w.trim().length > 0);\n      if (words.length === 0) return cap;\n\n      let bestWord 
= words[0];\n      let maxScore = -100;\n\n      words.forEach((w, index) => {\n        let score = w.length; \n       
 \n        if (index === words.length - 1) score += 3; // Punchline bonus\n        if (index === 0) score += 1; // 
Start word bonus\n        \n        if (w.match(/[A-Z]/)) {\n          if (w === w.toUpperCase()) {\n            score 
+= 5; // All caps bonus\n          } else {\n            score += 2; // Title case bonus\n          }\n        }\n     
   \n        if (w.length <= 2) score -= 10; // Penalize stop words strongly\n        if (w.length >= 7) score += 2; 
// Reward long descriptive words\n\n        if (score > maxScore) {\n          maxScore = score;\n          bestWord = 
w;\n        }\n      });\n      \n      const cleanImportant = bestWord.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, 
'').toLowerCase().trim();\n      let bestIndex = -1;\n      words.forEach((w, i) => {\n        if (w === bestWord && 
bestIndex === -1) {\n          bestIndex = i;\n        }\n      });\n      return { \n        ...cap, \n        
highlightedWords: cleanImportant ? [cleanImportant] : [],\n        highlightedIndices: bestIndex !== -1 ? [bestIndex] 
: [],\n        originalHighlightedWords: cleanImportant ? [cleanImportant] : [],\n        originalHighlightedIndices: 
bestIndex !== -1 ? [bestIndex] : []\n      };\n    });\n    setCaptions(newCaptions);\n  };\n\n  const 
loadFromTimeline = React.useCallback(() => {\n    fetch('/auto.srt?t=' + Date.now()) // cache bust\n      .then(res => 
res.text())\n      .then(text => {\n        if (text) {\n           const parsed = parseSrt(text);\n           const 
merged = parsed.map(newCap => {\n             const oldCap = captions.find(c => \n               c.id === newCap.id || 
Math.abs(c.startTime - newCap.startTime) < 1000\n             );\n             if (oldCap) {\n               return 
{\n                 ...newCap,\n                 highlightedWords: oldCap.highlightedWords || [],\n                 
highlightedIndices: oldCap.highlightedIndices || [],\n                 customStyle: oldCap.customStyle\n               
};\n             }\n             return newCap;\n           });\n           setCaptions(merged);\n           
window.history.replaceState({}, '', window.location.pathname);\n        }\n      })\n      .catch(err => 
console.error(err));\n  }, [setCaptions, captions]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!hasHydrated) return; // Wait for 
store to load from localStorage first!\n    \n    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);\n    
if (urlParams.get('autoLoad') === 'true') {\n      const fpsParam = urlParams.get('fps');\n      if (fpsParam) {\n     
   setVideoData(videoUrl || '', videoDuration || 0, parseFloat(fpsParam));\n      }\n      loadFromTimeline();\n    
}\n  }, [loadFromTimeline, setVideoData, videoUrl, videoDuration, hasHydrated]);\n\n  const maxCanvasTime = 
captions.length > 0 ? captions[captions.length - 1].endTime : 0;\n  \n  let durationInFrames = 300; // Default 10 
seconds\n  if (videoDuration > 0) {\n    durationInFrames = Math.max(1, Math.round((videoDuration / 1000) * fps));\n  
} else if (maxCanvasTime > 0) {\n    durationInFrames = Math.max(1, Math.round((maxCanvasTime / 1000) * fps));\n  
}\n\n  // Helper to load video metadata\n  const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n   
 if (videoUrl && videoRef.current) {\n      videoRef.current.src = videoUrl;\n      videoRef.current.onloadedmetadata 
= () => {\n        // Update duration in store (in ms)\n        setVideoData(videoUrl, videoRef.current!.duration * 
1000, fps);\n      };\n    }\n  }, [videoUrl, fps, setVideoData]);\n\n  const [isRendering, setIsRendering] = 
useState(false);\n  const [renderProgress, setRenderProgress] = useState(0);\n  const [downloadUrl, setDownloadUrl] = 
useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [isClient, setIsClient] = useState(false);\n  const [isLooping, setIsLooping] 
= useState(true);\n  const [confirmAction, setConfirmAction] = useState<{type: 'reload' | 'auto', open: boolean}>({ 
type: 'reload', open: false });\n\n  const playerRef = useRef<PlayerRef>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let 
animationFrameId: number;\n    const updateActiveCaption = () => {\n      if (playerRef.current && captions.length > 
0) {\n        const frame = playerRef.current.getCurrentFrame();\n        const timeMs = (frame / fps) * 1000;\n       
 \n        captions.forEach(cap => {\n          const el = document.getElementById(`caption-item-${cap.id}`);\n        
  if (el) {\n            const isActive = timeMs >= cap.startTime && timeMs <= cap.endTime;\n            if (isActive) 
{\n              el.style.borderColor = '#6366f1'; \n              el.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(49, 46, 129, 
0.4)';\n              el.style.boxShadow = '0 0 10px rgba(99,102,241,0.2)';\n            } else {\n              
el.style.borderColor = '';\n              el.style.backgroundColor = '';\n              el.style.boxShadow = '';\n     
       }\n          }\n        });\n      }\n      animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(updateActiveCaption);\n    
};\n    updateActiveCaption();\n    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId);\n  }, [captions, fps]);\n\n  
useEffect(() => {\n    setTimeout(() => setIsClient(true), 0);\n  }, []);\n\n  const handleRender = async () => {\n    
if (captions.length === 0) return;\n    setIsRendering(true);\n    setRenderProgress(0);\n    setDownloadUrl(null);\n  
  playerRef.current?.pause();\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('/api/render', {\n        method: 'POST',\n  
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          inputProps: {\n      
      videoUrl,\n            captions,\n            styleConfig,\n            fps\n          }\n        })\n      
});\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.jobId) {\n        pollStatus(data.jobId);\n      } else {\n  
      console.error('Render API Error:', data.error);\n        alert('Render failed to start: ' + (data.error || 
'Unknown error'));\n        setIsRendering(false);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(err);\n      
alert('Network error while starting render');\n      setIsRendering(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const pollStatus = async 
(jobId: string) => {\n    const interval = setInterval(async () => {\n      const res = await 
fetch(`/api/render?jobId=${jobId}`);\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.status === 'processing') 
{\n        setRenderProgress(data.progress);\n      } else if (data.status === 'done') {\n        
setRenderProgress(100);\n        setDownloadUrl(data.url);\n        setIsRendering(false);\n        
clearInterval(interval);\n        window.location.hash = `importMediaPool=${data.url}`;\n      } else if (data.status 
=== 'failed') {\n        setIsRendering(false);\n        clearInterval(interval);\n        alert('Render failed: ' + 
(data.error || 'Unknown error'));\n      }\n    }, 2000);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex flex-col 
lg:flex-row min-h-screen lg:h-screen lg:overflow-hidden overflow-y-auto bg-black text-white p-4 gap-6 relative\">\n    
  {/* Invisible video element to grab metadata */}\n      <video ref={videoRef} className=\"hidden\" />\n\n      {/* 
Left Sidebar: Captions, Render */}\n      {isLeftPanelOpen && (\n        <div className=\"w-full lg:w-80 flex-shrink-0

            type=\"checkbox\" \n                checked={highlightSimilar}\n                onChange={(e) =>

onClick={() => {\n                  setIndividualStylingEnabled(!individualStylingEnabled);\n                  if

</button>\n            </div>\n            \n\n          </div>\n          \n          <div className=\"space-y-2\">\n

        \n              return (\n              <div \n                id={`caption-item-${cap.id}`}\n

const midTime = cap.startTime + (cap.endTime - cap.startTime) / 2;\n                    const frameToSeek =

               }}\n                className={`p-3 rounded-lg border transition-all ${\n                  isSelected 
\n                    ? 'bg-indigo-900/60 border-indigo-400 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(99,102,241,0.3)] cursor-default' \n  
                  : individualStylingEnabled \n                      ? 'bg-gray-800 border-gray-700 
hover:border-indigo-500/50 cursor-pointer'\n                      : 'bg-gray-800 border-gray-700/50 
hover:border-indigo-500/30 cursor-pointer'\n                }`}\n              >\n                <div

                  e.stopPropagation(); \n                          setEditingCaptionId(cap.id); \n                     
     setEditingCaptionText(cap.text); \n                        }}\n                        className=\"text-gray-500

             <Edit2 className=\"w-3 h-3\" />\n                      </button>\n                    )}\n                
  </div>\n                  {hasCustomStyle && (\n                    <span className=\"text-[10px] bg-indigo-600

   \n                {editingCaptionId === cap.id ? (\n                  <div className=\"mt-2 flex flex-col 
gap-2\">\n                    <textarea \n                      value={editingCaptionText}\n                      
onChange={(e) => setEditingCaptionText(e.target.value)}\n                      className=\"w-full bg-gray-900

resize-none\"\n                      rows={2}\n                      autoFocus\n                    />\n               
     <div className=\"flex justify-end gap-2\">\n                      <button \n                        onClick={(e)

hover:bg-gray-600 flex items-center gap-1 text-xs rounded text-white\"\n                      >\n                      
  <X className=\"w-3 h-3\" /> Cancel\n                      </button>\n                      <button \n                
        onClick={(e) => { \n                          e.stopPropagation(); \n                          
updateCaptionSegment(cap.id, { text: editingCaptionText });\n                          setEditingCaptionId(null); \n   
                     }}\n                        className=\"px-2 py-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-500 flex

               ) : (\n                  <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-200 leading-relaxed flex flex-wrap gap-1

word.replace(/[.,!?;:\"'(){}[\\\\]\\\\-]/g, '').toLowerCase().trim();\n                    const isHighlighted =

<span\n                        key={i}\n                        onClick={(e) => {\n                          
e.stopPropagation(); // prevent selecting the block if clicking a word\n                          
toggleHighlight(cap.id, word, i);\n                        }}\n                        className={`cursor-pointer 
px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded transition-colors ${\n                          isHighlighted \n                            ? 
'bg-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300 font-medium' \n                            : 'hover:bg-gray-700'\n                   
     }`}\n                      >\n                        {word}\n                      </span>\n                    
);\n                  })}\n                </p>\n                )}\n              </div>\n              );\n          
  })}\n            {captions.length === 0 && (\n              <div className=\"text-sm text-gray-500 text-center

</div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"p-4 border-t border-gray-800\">\n          <button \n

Final Video'}\n          </button>\n          {downloadUrl && (\n            <a\n              href={downloadUrl}\n    
          download=\"Auto-Caps-Style-render.mov\"\n              className=\"bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-500

    </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Main Preview Area */}\n      <div className=\"flex-1 w-full min-h-[50vh] lg:min-h-0 
bg-gray-950 flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-4 lg:p-8 border border-gray-800 rounded-xl relative\">\n       
 {!isLeftPanelOpen && (\n          <button onClick={() => setIsLeftPanelOpen(true)} className=\"absolute top-4 left-4

       {!isRightPanelOpen && (\n          <button onClick={() => setIsRightPanelOpen(true)} className=\"absolute top-4
